***мара.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мара.html>ма́ра</a> (9454)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">mara</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:мара.html>ма́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="be-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mára</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:мара.html>ма́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:мара.html>ма́ры</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dream <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">hope or wish</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="be">мро́я</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="tr Latn">mrója</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:марать.html>мара́ть</a> (23886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марать.html>мара́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">marátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замарать.html>замара́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">намара́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soil, to stain, to dirty, to smut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:марать.html>мара́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>marátʹ</b> bumágu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">waste paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:марать.html>мара́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>marátʹ</b> rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">soil one's hands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sully, to stain, to tarnish, to blemish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замарать.html>замара́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:репутация.html>репута́цию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamarátʹ</b> reputáciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sully one's reputation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to daub, to scribble</li></ol>

***мариновать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мариновать.html>маринова́ть</a> (12347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marin(er)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мариновать.html>маринова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">marinovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замаринова́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to marinate, to pickle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to delay, to shelve, to put off, to keep waiting, to keep, to make languish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:марля.html>ма́рля</a> (18484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marli</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gauze, muslin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марс.html>марс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mars</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марс.html>ма́рса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марс.html>ма́рсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марс.html>ма́рсов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> top <i>(on sailing vessels, a platform around the head of a lower mast)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crow's nest <i>(observation platform at the top of a ship’s mast)</i></li></ol>

***марсианский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:марсианский.html>марсиа́нский</a> (20853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
